–∞, —è —Ç–∞–º —Å–æ–∫—Ä–∞—â–∞–ª, —á—Ç–æ –± –Ω–µ –≥—Ä—É–∑–∏—Ç—å
$gd_kit_ws_status $mol_view
  attr *
    ^
    gd_kit_ws_status <= status \connecting
    title <= hint \
  minimal_width 40
  minimal_height 40
  hint_prefix \Socket
  ws $gd_kit_ws
  sub /$mol_view
    <= Icon $mol_view
  status_icon *
    error <= Error_icon $mol_icon_sync_off
    connecting <= Connecting_icon $mol_icon_sync_alert
    open <= Open_icon $mol_icon_sync
    checked <= Checked_icon $mol_icon_cloud_sync


namespace $.$$ {
  export class $gd_kit_ws_status extends $.$gd_kit_ws_status {
    @ $mol_mem
    override status() {
      return this.ws().status()
    }

    override Icon() {
      const icons = this.status_icon()
      const status = this.status()
      return status ? icons[status] : icons.error
    }

    override hint() {
      const error = this.ws().error()?.val.message

      return `${this.hint_prefix()} ${this.status()}${(error ? ` [${error}]` : '')}`
    }

  }
}

Sergey Yuferev 
  export class $gd_kit_cursor<Item = string, Criteria = string> extends $mol_object {
    @ $mol_mem_key
    after_fetch(criteria: Criteria, next?: readonly Item[]): readonly Item[] {
      throw new Error('implement')
    }

    @ $mol_mem_key
    after(criteria: Criteria, next?: readonly Item[]) {
      this.fetched.add(criteria)
      return this.after_fetch(criteria, next)
    }

    protected fetched = new Set<Criteria>()

    distance(a: Criteria, b: Criteria): number {
      throw new Error('implement')
    }

    nearest_chunk(criteria: Criteria): readonly Item[] | undefined {
      let chunk = undefined as undefined | readonly Item[]

      let distance = Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY
      let nearest: Criteria | undefined = undefined

      for (const fetched_criteria of this.fetched) {
        const dist = this.distance(fetched_criteria, criteria)
        if (dist > distance) continue
        distance = dist
        nearest = fetched_criteria
      }

      return nearest ? this.after(nearest) : undefined
    }

    tmp_after_add(criteria: Criteria, item: Item) {
      const chunk = this.nearest_chunk(criteria)
      if (! chunk) return
      this.after(criteria, [ ...chunk, item ])
    }
  }

11:31 
  export class $gd_kit_cursor<Item = string, Criteria = string> extends $mol_object {
    @ $mol_mem_key
    before(criteria: Criteria): readonly Item[] {
      throw new Error('implement')
    }

    @ $mol_mem_key
    after(criteria: Criteria): readonly Item[] {
      throw new Error('implement')
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    rows(next?: readonly Item[]) {
      return next ?? []
    }

    compare(a: Item, b: Item): number {
      throw new Error('implement')
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    criteria_desc()  {
      const rows = this.rows()
      return rows.some(row => this.compare(rows[0], row) > 0)
    }

    insert(item: Item) {
      const rows = this.rows()
      let i = 0

      if (this.criteria_desc()) {
        i = rows.length - 1
        for (; i >= 0; i--) {
          if (this.compare(item, rows[i]) < 0) break
        }
        if (i < 0) i = 0
      } else {
        for (; i < rows.length; i++) {
          if (this.compare(item, rows[i]) < 0) break
        }
      }


      this.rows(rows.toSpliced(i, 0, item))
    }
}
